<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_725a5ab7-b1b6-41c8-8a05-dd0217f1dfb1'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText17033074937784555587" style="display:none"><i>Librarian's Note: This is an alternate cover for ASIN# B00BT0JB0A</i><br /><br /><b>A <i>USA Today</i> bestselling book. <i>Leo</i> is a full-length, standalone romance.</b><br /><br />Evie and Leo met in foster care as children and formed a bond of friendship. As they grew, their bond turned to love, and they vowed to make a life together when they turned 18 and were no longer a part of the system.<br /><br />When Leo unexpectedly gets adopted as a teen and moves to another city, he promises Evie that he will contact her as soon as he gets there and come back for her in a few short years. She never hears from him again.<br /><br />Now eight years later, in spite of the odds, Evie has made a life for herself. She has a job. She has friends. She's content. Then a man shows up out of the blue, claiming that her long lost love, Leo, sent him to check up on her. The attraction between them is undeniable. But, should she trust this sexy stranger? Or is he keeping a secret about what his connection to Leo is really all about and why Leo disappeared all those years ago?<br /><br />THIS IS A STANDALONE SIGN OF LOVE NOVEL, INSPIRED BY LEO. New Adult Contemporary Romance: Due to strong language and sexual content, this book is not intended for readers under the age of 18.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer561600737" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17625329924020564100"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413458i/814117._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> SQUEEEE!!! OMG I have so many feels for this book!!!!! <br/><br/>Everything about this story was beautiful!! ♥♥♥<br/><br/>It me cry, laugh, swoon and fan myself and honestly, I just loved it all!! </b><br/><br/>This is a spoiler-free review. 4.5 - 5 stars.<br/><br/><blockquote> <i>“The thing about falling in love so that no matter where you are when it happens, you can’t help but to color those moments with beauty, even if you’re in a location of ugliness. He made what would have been a place of nightmares into a place to dream.” </i>
</blockquote> <br/>Second-chance love s</span>
  <span id="freeText17625329924020564100" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413458i/814117._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> SQUEEEE!!! OMG I have so many feels for this book!!!!! <br><br>Everything about this story was beautiful!! ♥♥♥<br><br>It me cry, laugh, swoon and fan myself and honestly, I just loved it all!! </b><br><br>This is a spoiler-free review. 4.5 - 5 stars.<br><br><blockquote> <i>“The thing about falling in love so that no matter where you are when it happens, you can’t help but to color those moments with beauty, even if you’re in a location of ugliness. He made what would have been a place of nightmares into a place to dream.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>Second-chance love stories are my favorite but one’s with a cool twist are just a bonus. This is the kind of book that makes you want to re-read it, or at least certain parts of it. There is just so much to the story that you can only fully appreciate after having gone through all the big reveals… and knowing them just gives so much *more* to the story, so it’s going on my re-read pile for sure <br><br>Now, I know it’s only 192 pages long but honestly, it didn’t feel short at all. The story was never rushed and the ending wrapped up beautifully with a happy-tear-enducing epilogue. And sometimes you just WANT a really wonderful book that you can read in one sitting, you know? <br><br>The story starts out in a flashback. Evie is 14, Leo is 15. They met in the first foster home they were placed and became the best of friends. They relied on each other, bonded, and as they grew older, that developed into love. He was <i> “the boy who makes me want to stay awake because reality is finally better than my dreams.” </i><br><br>But when Leo gets adopted by a family across the country, they are forced apart. They make vows and he promises to come back for her when they turn 18… but that is the last time she sees him.<br><br>Eight years later, Evie has forged a life for herself. Despite having grown up in a life without family, filled with drugs, molestation and bad memories, she is strong, self sufficient and has gotten a job, a little home for herself, and generally has everything under control. She has moved on from the hurt of her past but has never forgotten what she felt for Leo. So when a guy shows up one day who says that Leo sent him to check on her, it just throws her world. She feels pulled towards him somehow but there is something mysterious about him and his connection to Leo… and she has to decide whether or not she can trust him…<br><br>I was feeling the emotion right from the start of the book. By page 2, I already wanted to cry. The first scene of the book, which was also the scene of their first kiss/goodbye when Leo got adopted just made my heart HURT even though I barely knew them… definitely one of the most beautifully written first kisses ever!!<br><br><blockquote> <i> <b> “I’m going to kiss you now, Evie, and when I do, it’s going to mean that you’re mine. I don’t care how far away we are from each other. You. Are. Mine. I’ll wait for you. And I want you to wait for me. Promise me…” </b></i>
</blockquote>  <br><br>If that quote doesn’t make you want to read the book, I don’t know what will! From that line on, I was hooked! ♥<br><br>I loved the writing. It drew you right into the story and I felt totally connected to everything that happened. It was fast paced without being rushed and flowed very smoothly. It slowed down in the important parts of the scene but I loved that the story was constantly moving forward and adding more pieces to the puzzle.<br><br>It was told in back and forth flashbacks and present day…. but with the way the story was woven, it left me unable to put it down. I alternated between heart clenching during the flashbacks and swooning over the present day parts.<br><br>I have to say though that I read with a complete mixture of swoon and suspicion. I *knew* something was up, I just KNEW it but I couldn’t put my finger on what it was. I had theories and it kept me guessing….<br><br>And so when the big reveal happened, I had to read it twice. The first time was just in shock (call me naive but I did not see it coming!) and I just got these huge chills and shivers and had to stop and go back and read that page again and then I just started to cry. Oh. My. God…. incredible scene!!!!<br><br>I just looooved the twist! It explained and connected everything perfectly! But then… hmmm once the full explanation came out, I had to think a little about how that made me feel about the character. But the more I read, the more understanding I became. It didn’t make what happened okay in my eyes, but people make mistakes and they mess up. Nobody is perfect. And if they get to a point where you kind of have to choose to accept them or not and there was no doubt in my eyes that I wanted to accept.<br><br>I also wanted to add in that, despite the fact that this story is told from Evie’s POV, the author has an awesome way of describing the male characters in these little subtle ways (narrowing of the eyes, clenching of the jaw, raking a hand through the hair… ) that just added extra yum to them and I found myself reading a lot with a little half smile on my face.<br><br>I’d classify this book somewhere between New Adult and Adult, maybe closer to adult. There is certainly steam and there are several hot hot hot scenes that are rather descriptive so that’s what’s leaning me towards Adult. That being said, I thought the steam was very well done because the story took the time to FIRST develop the connection with the characters so that by the time they got into bed, you were feeling emotionally connected to them.<br><br><b> The ending is fully resolved and very swoony. No cliffhanger, guys!!! </b><br><br>And, as a bonus, we get an absolutely gorgeous epilogue. Seriously, bless the hearts of every author who writes an epilogue. If I could hug them all, I would. That extra piece to the story just adds that last little bit that puts your heart to rest about the future of the characters you’ve fallen in love with. And this epilogue was particularly heart melting – it was the perfect conclusion to their story.<br><br><b> Overall, LEO is a beautiful, well-written, swoony and emotional read with steam, a bit of mystery and a happy ending ♥ </b><br><br><blockquote> <i>“I can’t make the fire go away,” she had seemed to say. “I can’t guarantee you won’t get burned. But… I can remain steady and strong, because I believe in you. Because you are mine.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>I’d highly recommend it and am adding it to my list of <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com/best-books-of-2013/" rel="nofollow noopener">Best Books of 2013</a>.<br><br>4.5 – 5 stars.<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413458i/814118._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>BLURB --&gt; <i> Evie and Leo met in foster care as children and formed a bond of friendship. As they grew, their bond turned to love and they vowed to make a life together when they turned 18 and were no longer a part of the system.<br><br>When Leo unexpectedly gets adopted as a teen and he moves to another city, he promises Evie that he will contact her as soon as he gets there and come back for her in a few short years. She never hears from him again.<br><br>Now eight years later, in spite of the odds, Evie has made a life for herself. She has a job, she has friends, she's content. Then a man shows up out of the blue, claiming that her long lost love, Leo, sent him to check up on her. The attraction between them is undeniable. But, should she trust this sexy stranger? Or is he keeping a secret about what his connection to Leo is really all about and why Leo disappeared all those years ago? </i><br><br>New Adult Contemporary Romance: Due to strong language and sexual content, this book is not intended for readers under the age of 18.(less)<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17625329924020564100" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <b>WOW WOW WOW 4.5 STARS!!!!!!</b>

But I was sucked into this story in a second! <br/>I don't think t</span>
  <span id="freeText2284210844526638815" style="display:none">*ARC given to me by author in exchange for an honest review*<br><br><b>
  <i>“And in the end, I had jumped. And the other side was just as glorious as her eyes had promised“</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>WOW WOW WOW 4.5 STARS!!!!!!</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I must confess that I did not expect to love this book so much. In the beginning I had some trouble how the main female character takes slightly the idea of someone following her and not thinking that that is something you should report to police! But I was sucked into this story in a second! <br>I don't think there are many of books in which I love both main characters, usually SHE is annoying to me but this girl... i loved her from the beginning!<br>I must also admit that the style how it was written did remind me of KA's book CREED but honestly to me it was even better, much softer and CREED I really liked!<br><br><b>THE STORY </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413076i/812906.jpg" width="500" height="333" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Evie and Leo met around age 10 in foster care, both having ugly childhood. Soon they become best friends and he becomes her protector. They plan leaving together when they both turn 18 but one day Leo gets adopted and moves to another city leaving her alone but promising her he will come back for her. She promises to wait but he doesn't come back to save her on her 18th birthday.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413076ra/812907.gif" width="500" height="281" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"I'm going to kiss you now, Evie, and when I do, it's going to mean that you're mine. I<br>don't care how far away from each other we are. You. Are. Mine. I'll wait for you. And I want you to<br>wait for me. Promise me you won't let anyone else touch you. Promise me you'll save yourself for me."</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413076ra/812908.gif" width="500" height="226" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story beginns with Evie realizing someone is stalking her for a week, having really bad childhood and learning how to survive on streets, she doesn't feel threatened and decides to confront her stalker. <br><br>And here enters <b>JAKE MADSEN &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3 </b><br><br>Four years after her 18th birthday she finds out that Leo died in a car accident a year ago, even though she doesn't want to feel the sorrow because he never wrote her in all those years, she can't help but feel betrayed...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413076ra/812909.gif" width="500" height="385" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jake promised to Leo to check if she is alright and in the week he was following her he fell in love.<br><br><b>OMG!!! JAKE MADSEN!!!!! NOW THAT IS A NAME YOU WILL REMEMBER!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413076ra/812910.gif" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Jake is full of secrets from the beginning, even when he tells her something, he really does not say anything that she wants to know but the only thing that he tells her for sure is that he has every intent to make her his.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Evie," he says quietly, finally looking at me, "What I mean is, when I fuck you, you're going to be mine. Is that clear enough for you?"</i>
</b><br><br>Jake as an 25 year old is extremely alpha and when you read about him you really don't have a feeling he is that young. He is very delicious, very mysterious, protective and possessive but every time the opportunity to destroy them as a couple knocks on their door he falls apart and you can see how much he is hurting and trying to tell her his dark secrets but doesn't know how to because with that he might loose her forever.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413076i/812911._SY540_.jpg" width="415" height="538" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>''He leans his forehead against mine and looks right into my eyes. There is an unreadable expression there and my heart starts to beat faster as we stare at each other, mere centimeters away. I don't know whether I'm scared or whether his closeness is causing my blood to pump faster. I don't know what I'm feeling in this moment, don't know whether I want to move even closer or pull away''</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413076i/812912.jpg" width="500" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Now I must admitt that the hot parts with them were <b>EXTREMELY HOT!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413076ra/812913.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413076ra/812914.gif" width="450" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>But to keep someone you want in your life, those secrets need to come out...<br>All you need to do is jump and have faith....</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413076ra/812915.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3043997854?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="jessica" href="/user/show/10171516-jessica">jessica</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3043997854" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15024299545291756912">oh my goodness. what a tender story, one that really makes me believe in the goodness and beauty that can be found in humanity. <br/><br/>i had a great upbringing with two parents who loved me and made sure i had exactly what i needed, nothing more and nothing less. i went on to get a good education and currently have a job that i enjoy. my background couldnt be any more different than leo and evies. but if two people who have had to experience the crappy hand life has dealt them can still came out in the</span>
  <span id="freeText15024299545291756912" style="display:none">oh my goodness. what a tender story, one that really makes me believe in the goodness and beauty that can be found in humanity. <br /><br />i had a great upbringing with two parents who loved me and made sure i had exactly what i needed, nothing more and nothing less. i went on to get a good education and currently have a job that i enjoy. my background couldnt be any more different than leo and evies. but if two people who have had to experience the crappy hand life has dealt them can still came out in the end full of love and compassion, well, then thats something to really admire. <br /><br />i know this book is fiction, but their story is not. i believe that people have the capability to be never lose hope in the face of adversity, that kindness can be used as an effective coping mechanism, and that believing in someone (especially when they dont believe in themselves) is the kind of loyalty and support everyone deserves.<br /><br />so dont let the cheesy outdated cover fool you because this story is sooo much more. <br /><br /><b>↠ <i>5 stars</i></b></span>

<div id="review_563088941" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/563088941" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/563088941?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17608346-leo">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer563088941" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11975957006388531977"><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“No matter how far apart we are. No matter the distance or time, I will never love anyone except you. Not ever.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/>My <b>EVIE</b> and <b>LEO</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/8226cf23-896c-4396-aec5-59c07c21498b_zps675ce595.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814850._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 8226cf23-896c-4396-aec5-59c07c21498b_zps675ce595.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/59239986-c93f-4517-9dfc-32d8c4709587_zpsf29236c3.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814851.jpg' alt=' photo 59239986-c93f-4517-9dfc-32d8c4709587_zpsf29236c3.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is a story about Evie and Leo. Two kids who met when Evie was 10 and Leo was 11...<br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>We met in the first foster care home each of us were sent to and he’s my best friend in the world, the boy I’ve grown to love.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/fc3bbb38-9e15-4850-9816-9f298be5af7e_zps9c31dd12.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814852.jpg' alt=' photo fc3bbb38-9e15-4850-9816-9f298be5af7e_zps9c31dd12.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Leo and Evie become the best of friends. As they get a little older, they fall in love. When Leo is 15 and Evie is 14, Leo g</span>
  <span id="freeText11975957006388531977" style="display:none"><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“No matter how far apart we are. No matter the distance or time, I will never love anyone except you. Not ever.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>My <b>EVIE</b> and <b>LEO</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/8226cf23-896c-4396-aec5-59c07c21498b_zps675ce595.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814850._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 8226cf23-896c-4396-aec5-59c07c21498b_zps675ce595.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/59239986-c93f-4517-9dfc-32d8c4709587_zpsf29236c3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814851.jpg" alt=" photo 59239986-c93f-4517-9dfc-32d8c4709587_zpsf29236c3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is a story about Evie and Leo. Two kids who met when Evie was 10 and Leo was 11...<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>We met in the first foster care home each of us were sent to and he’s my best friend in the world, the boy I’ve grown to love.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/fc3bbb38-9e15-4850-9816-9f298be5af7e_zps9c31dd12.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814852.jpg" alt=" photo fc3bbb38-9e15-4850-9816-9f298be5af7e_zps9c31dd12.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Leo and Evie become the best of friends. As they get a little older, they fall in love. When Leo is 15 and Evie is 14, Leo gets adopted and has to move to SanDiego, across the country from where Evie. is. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/690d1c2b-dc72-4f68-9de4-e9f241365077_zps33108d42.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814853.jpg" alt=" photo 690d1c2b-dc72-4f68-9de4-e9f241365077_zps33108d42.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Leo makes a promise to Evie. He will wait for her, she will wait for him. In four years, when she turns 18, he will come for her. They can start to live their life together. He will write, call etc. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/9f978356-367f-49f9-ac6f-40560bb05d3f_zps30dc0708.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814854.jpg" alt=" photo 9f978356-367f-49f9-ac6f-40560bb05d3f_zps30dc0708.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Evie lives up to her end of the bargain, but she never hears from Leo again. She is upset, worried, hurt, but she moves on with her life. She tries not to think to much about him, but 8 years later, one of Leo’s friends contacts her. Jake. Jake tells Evie he knew Leo from college, Leo was in a car accident and didn’t make it. But he asked Jake to check on her. This is really hard for Evie to hear. <br><br>Evie feels something for Jake. Something she has never felt for another man, except Leo. Jake asks her out and she accepts. Jake runs his family’s business, has a lot of money, and lives in a nice condo. Evie works two jobs, one as maid and the other, a caterer to make rent on her studio apt. But there is something about Evie. Jake is enamored with her. He wants to know all about her, but he doesn’t share much about himself. They grow close. Jake is a dominate, possessive, alpha male. He is a known ladies man, Evie is very inexperienced. She doesn't know for sure if she can trust Jake, but she wants to. They are happy together. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/0089bcfa-5b6a-453a-a26a-ae0a41c40fdc_zpsce6bce0d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814855.jpg" alt=" photo 0089bcfa-5b6a-453a-a26a-ae0a41c40fdc_zpsce6bce0d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jake has secrets. When they come to light, it will change everything between these two. <br><br>Okay- my take: I really liked this one. It was a shorter read, but good. I spent a lot of the book trying to figure out why... why didn’t Leo contact Evie, what is Jake hiding? When I read the ‘twist’ of the story, I was a little shocked, a little sad, but also happy. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/1b37683c-0c2e-4ef4-8789-fd678aeeaf60_zps8793e6fd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814856.jpg" alt=" photo 1b37683c-0c2e-4ef4-8789-fd678aeeaf60_zps8793e6fd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>All the flashbacks with Leo, that was one of my favorite parts of the story. I loved seeing Evie and Leo’s relationship. Leo was the sweetest. I hate what he had to go through as a child. The stories with his brother broke my heart. Evie didn’t have it easy either. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I went through a lot to get where I am and I don’t take anything I have for granted, ever. That’s my reward.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Evie is independent. She is sweet, kind, compassionate and polite. She has had a hard life, but hasn’t let that life turn her hard. She is happy with what she has accomplished, and doesn’t take anything for granted. She was a great heroine. <br><br>It was also cool that this story took place 10 miles from where I live :D <br>The ending was fantastic, I loved the epilogue! <br>A solid 4-4.5 stars from me! I would definitely recommend this one! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/ef461c63-410a-4d50-afcb-cee1a4d28613_zps1b1e65d2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413674i/814857.jpg" alt=" photo ef461c63-410a-4d50-afcb-cee1a4d28613_zps1b1e65d2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“Everyone tells a story about themselves in their own head. That story makes you what you are, dictating all your actions and all your mistakes. If your own story is filled with guilt and fear and self-hatred, life can look pretty miserable. But, if you're very lucky, you might have a person who tells you a better story, one that takes up residence in your soul, speaking louder than the woeful tale you've convinced yourself of. If you let it speak loudly within your heart, it becomes your passion and your purpose.” </i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_559344085" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559344085" />
    <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha"><img alt="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528597635p2/15735368.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559344085?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SueBee★bring me an alpha!★" href="/user/show/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha">SueBee★bring me an alpha!★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=read-stand-alones-cr">read-stand-alones-cr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=heroes-troubled-tortured">heroes-troubled-tortured</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=read-contemporaries">read-contemporaries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=series-check-on-sequel">series-check-on-sequel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=series-g-contemporaries">series-g-contemporaries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=g-contemporaries">g-contemporaries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=4-and-half-stars">4-and-half-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=heroes-rich-all">heroes-rich-all</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15735368-suebee-bring-me-an-alpha?shelf=heroes-rich-heir-tycoon-modern">heroes-rich-heir-tycoon-modern</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559344085" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17344925083858737113"><b>★★★★1/2! Sign of Love series, book 1 (Stand-alone) Debut by Mia Sheridan. An amazing heroine & a bossy alpha male with a troubled past are brought together by the loss of a friend.</b><br/><br/><i>This is book 1 in the Sign of Love series. Based on this book’s ending I have concluded that this is a stand-alone series, but this has not been confirmed by the author yet.</i><br/><br/><b>Hero: <u>Jake (Jacob) Madsen</u>/business owner-mogul/$$$/23 years old/light brown hair/brown eyes/6’2”<br/>Heroine: <u>Evelyn Cruise, Evie</u>/hotel maid-part time c</b></span>
  <span id="freeText17344925083858737113" style="display:none"><b>★★★★1/2! Sign of Love series, book 1 (Stand-alone) Debut by Mia Sheridan. An amazing heroine &amp; a bossy alpha male with a troubled past are brought together by the loss of a friend.</b><br /><br /><i>This is book 1 in the Sign of Love series. Based on this book’s ending I have concluded that this is a stand-alone series, but this has not been confirmed by the author yet.</i><br /><br /><b>Hero: <u>Jake (Jacob) Madsen</u>/business owner-mogul/$$$/23 years old/light brown hair/brown eyes/6’2”<br />Heroine: <u>Evelyn Cruise, Evie</u>/hotel maid-part time caterer/22 years old/dark brown hair/brown eyes/5’5”</b><br /><br />Jake and Evie are brought together when Jake seeks her out to deliver the news that her childhood friend and first love, Leo has died in a car accident. But even though this book opens up with such tragic news we’re quickly pulled into the story and the budding romance between Jake and Evie. This is their story!<br /><br />The memories of Leo will serve as a backdrop throughout the book with Evie reminiscing about her childhood. Leo and Evie met in the foster care system and became the closest of friends. When Leo was adopted and moved away his last promise was that he would come back for her on her 18th birthday and he had made her promise she’d wait for him. The glimpses into their past are very poignant, but also give us an understandings of who Evie is and why she would save herself for 8 years waiting on Leo. Here is their first meeting at age 10 and 11 respectively:<br /><br /><i>“This is Leo's first night here. Leo was in charge of putting the napkins out and I notice that he put them on the right and they're supposed to go on the left. I only know this because I like to read books like Ann of Green Gables, and Little House on the Prairie, and I pick up random things like that from the stories.”</i><br /><br />Evie is truly a wonderful heroine; she is smart and witty, beautiful and kind, loving and caring and so very strong. Despite everything that has happened to her she has persevered and managed to make a modest life for herself. She works two jobs with hopes of being able to attend college. She has aspirations of becoming a writer, but since she doesn’t own a computer she uses the computer at the library. She is the type of person who touches people’s heart. Chances are she will stay with you…<br /><i>
  <b>“It will only ever be you, Evie.”</b>
</i><br /><br />But she has a spunky, feisty side:<br /><i>“You don't know me. You think you do, but you don't. You think you know what type of person I am, but you have no idea. And so, you don't get to do this. You don't get to interrupt my life over and over again and then think that I will be grateful to you for gracing my life with your very presence…”</i><br /><br />Evie also has two wonderful friends in Nicole and Landon (aka the Cliché).<br /><br />Jake is has many of the characteristics I love in a hero. At first glance he is the bossy alpha male hero and he is handsome and sexy, successful and rich and he is quite taken with Evie. But as the story progresses we learn that there is more to Jake; He has secrets and we catch glimpses of a troubled hero. Add to that villains (scorned exes) set out to break them apart…. I will say no more because I want you to enjoy reading Jake’s and Evie’s story as much as I did.<br /><br />This was a quick read. And I really don’t have any complaints, other than I might have wished the book to be longer so ending could have been stretched over a longer period of time. That said I am content with how events unfolded. I loved every moment. An excellent debut by Mia Sheridan!<br /><br />There are moments of joy and butterflies, sexy hot moments with a very bossy Jake and then there are other moments of profound sadness… and reflection:<br /><br /><i>“Everyone tells a story about themselves in their own head. That story makes you what you are, dictating all your actions and all your mistakes. If your own story is filled with guilt and fear and self-hatred, life can look pretty miserable. But, if you're very lucky, you might have a person who tells you a better story, one that takes up residence in your soul, speaking louder than the woeful tale you've convinced yourself of. If you let it speak loudly within your heart, it becomes your passion and your purpose.”</i><br /><br />***<br />Hero rating: 4.5 stars <br />Heroine rating: 4.5 stars<br />Sex scenes rating: 4 stars<br />Sex scenes frequency: 4.5 stars<br />Storyline concept rating: 4.5 stars<br />Storytelling skills rating: 4.5 stars<br />Story ending rating: 4.5 stars<br />Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 5 stars<br />********************************************************<br /><b>Overall rating: 4.5 stars<br /><br />Would I recommend this book: Yes.<br />Would I re-read this book: Maybe later.<br />Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17344925083858737113" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_567163409" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/567163409" />
    <a title="Katie(babs)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs"><img alt="Katie(babs)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1242522005p2/179852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/567163409?book_show_action=true">Mar 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie(babs)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie(babs)" href="/user/show/179852-katie-babs">Katie(babs)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17608346-leo">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/179852-katie-babs?shelf=gag-worthy-book">gag-worthy-book</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer567163409" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13682090866484414864">Leo (Sign of Love #1) by Mia Sheridan had a great premise based on the blurb. It’s what I guess you would call a New Adult featuring a twenty-two year old woman named Evie who survived the horrors of foster care and has made a wonderful life for herself, but is still stuck on the young boy who made her feel special and not so alone. Evie first fell in love with Leo, who promised to keep in touch (he’s adopted at fifteen and moves across country) and come for her when she turns eighteen so they c</span>
  <span id="freeText13682090866484414864" style="display:none">Leo (Sign of Love #1) by Mia Sheridan had a great premise based on the blurb. It’s what I guess you would call a New Adult featuring a twenty-two year old woman named Evie who survived the horrors of foster care and has made a wonderful life for herself, but is still stuck on the young boy who made her feel special and not so alone. Evie first fell in love with Leo, who promised to keep in touch (he’s adopted at fifteen and moves across country) and come for her when she turns eighteen so they can be together forever. Leo was her protector and her soul mate, or so we’re led to believe from the beginning when Evie is fourteen and Leo is fifteen. Promises are made and kisses are exchanged. And then it’s eight years later and Evie is all alone. Leo disappeared ad was never heard from again.<br /><br />Evie was able to get her GED, finds work as a maid in a hotel and as a part time server for caterer. She has her own apartment and is making ends meet the best she can. She still wonders what happened to Leo and why he didn’t keep his promise to her. One day she realizes she’s being watched, or stalked, as she comes to think of it. She confronts her “stalker”, who’s a pretty handsome guy named Jake and forgives him for freaking her out. It appears Jake once knew Leo, who he has died in a car accident. Evie is extremely saddened that Leo died and wishes she could have said her goodbyes to the boy she holds near and dear to her heart. But there’s Jake, who’s new to the area and makes her feel warm inside. At twenty-three Jake’s in charge of his recently deceased father’s company, drives a BMW, has money to burn and the GQ looks. Jake wants to get to know Evie better, and soon he’s whisking her away on dates and treating her like a princess. Evie isn’t sure about Jake, but he’s protective, nice and treats her well. He respects her and her past feelings for Leo, going as far to admit she’s a virgin because she promised Leo she would wait for him. But now that Leo’s gone and Jake is in her life, she lets the memory of Leo go and welcomes Jake fully. She gives her body, heart and soul to this prince charming. But things seem too good to be true with Jake, and when she finds out what he’s hiding, she’s destroyed because has hew too good to be true lover has been lying to her all this time.<br /><br />Leo has a great beginning which crashes and burns immediately. This book is ridiculous to the point I was rolling my eyes throughout. It’s obvious this is a first time novel by Mia Sheridan because she makes all the mistakes a first time writer makes. Right from the start we have a massive amount of info dumping that doesn’t let up. Evie, the main protagonist is a stereotypical, been there, done that goodie goody who acts much younger than she is. Jake is only a year older than her and acts twice his age. What red blooded twenty-three year old male, regardless of their social status calls a woman a “minx” after they make love? Also Jake’s personality is all over the place. One moment he’s this alpha male, the next this self conscious, anxious young man that comes out of nowhere. Speaking of stereotypical characters, there’s a token sassy gay friend for Evie I found insulting (has it become a trope in New Adult to have a stereotypical sassy gay friend for the heroine?) and a skanky ex-girlfriend of Jake’s who warns Evie away from him, as well as Jake’s step-mother who’s a money grubbing, sexual piranha.<br /><br />This book is one big cliché in every way. Also it has a big young adult tone, more so than an adult one (maybe because Evie acts more like a thirteen year old) but when it comes to the sex, and there’s plenty, it’s over the top cheesiness. I felt like I was reading the first draft of a letter to Penthouse. Words like “shaft”, “clit” and “white cum” were used along with over the top purple prose. This quickly morphs into erotica and really doesn’t fit at all. It makes for a very uncomfortable reading experience. By the middle of the book it was all sex and badly written sex at that. The dialogue Jake speaks while intimate with Evie had me giggling, and not because it was meant to be funny. The love scenes here would make most romance readers close the book in disgust. Seriously, if you’re going to insert love scenes into a book, I would hope you’ve done some type of research on what sex feels like and how it should be portrayed. I felt the love scenes were a mish-mash of various love scenes written in other books.<br /><br />The mystery about Jake is very easy to figure out, and when he explains his past and his lies, that’s as comical as the cheesetastic sex he gives Evie. His story and how he turned out and why isn’t poignant or heartbreaking in any way.<br /><br />Honestly, nothing about this book from the characters to the story feels realistic. It’s tripe and again full of clichés and reads more like an experiment from a first time writer who wanted to write an emotional, almost epic romance but failed in every way. How it sold enough copies to make the USA Today list last week is a big mystery to me because this book is far from anything worthwhile or spectacular.<br /><br />A big pass on this one. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13682090866484414864" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1262979653" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1262979653" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1262979653?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=second-chance">second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1262979653" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7911636900626386302"><b>3.75 **<u>so sweet</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457367525i/18351465.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Why are you looking at me?”<br/>“Because I like your face.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This was such an exciting read for me. My very first <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6994378.Mia_Sheridan' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mia Sheridan</a> book. Now most of my friends suggested to start with some of her later works, but for those of you who know me I'm pretty peculiar and very insistent on reading in order. Without an actual series order I went with release date. So <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17825503-leo' rel='nofollow noopener'>Leo</a> it was. And what a sweet and moving book to get the ball rolling. A solid first book by Ms. Sheridan and some</span>
  <span id="freeText7911636900626386302" style="display:none"><b>3.75 **<u>so sweet</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457367525i/18351465.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Why are you looking at me?”<br>“Because I like your face.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This was such an exciting read for me. My very first <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6994378.Mia_Sheridan" rel="nofollow noopener">Mia Sheridan</a> book. Now most of my friends suggested to start with some of her later works, but for those of you who know me I'm pretty peculiar and very insistent on reading in order. Without an actual series order I went with release date. So <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17825503-leo" rel="nofollow noopener">Leo</a> it was. And what a sweet and moving book to get the ball rolling. A solid first book by Ms. Sheridan and something that made me very interested in more. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Maybe I’m an open book, or maybe love is like a magnifying glass straight into the souls of those who own your heart.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><i>Leo</i> tells the story of two kids who grew up in foster care. <b>Leo and Evie</b> first met when they were 11 and 10 years old. Stuck in a cruel system with no one to rely on but themselves. That was until they learned how to trust and support each other. A beautiful friendship grew into a strong and unmovable love. <br><br>Until one day when Evie was 14 years old Leo was suddenly adopted and had to move away. They promised to never lose their bond and stay connected until they could be together again. It's been eight years since Evie last heard from the love of her life and she lost hope long ago that she would ever see him again. <br><br>Evie did the best she could with her life, but for all intents and purposes she is stuck in suspended animation, still waiting for her soulmate and trying to improve her life little by little. That changed the day she confronts her ‘stalker’, the handsome and mysterious Jake. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“All the world's a circus. Sometimes you choose your act and sometimes it's assigned to you. I had roamed the arena for far too long, roaring and bellowing, believing that I wasn't brave enough to leap through fire. But all along, she had stood there, constant and calm.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm not going to lie, it was painfully obvious what was going on here. Nothing was really a big surprise. Despite some rather unexpected revelations towards the end the direction was clear from the start. And I didn't mind at all. The story was beautiful and heartwarming nevertheless. I enjoyed the writing, the carefully constructed characters and if you ae in the mood for a sweet and a little sexy second chance romance you should give this a try.<br><br>Since I’m writing this review after I already finished <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17801656-leo-s-chance" rel="nofollow noopener">Leo’s Chance</a>, the companion piece in Leo’s POV, I want to mention that I very much suggest reading the second book if you liked <i>Leo</i>. It is very rare that the same story written from different character's viewpoint gets my attention or better yet holds that attention long enough for me to finish reading.<br><br>I have to say it was a very well rounded and very enjoyable addition. For the most part I even think <i>Leo's Chance</i> was the better book overall, the writing was improved (if that is even possible) and Leo's voice was very strong and well developed. In hindsight the different vantage point was probably needed to really tell the story. <i>Leo’s Chance</i> didn’t really disclose anymore than <i>Leo</i> did, but it was a lot more emotional and gut wrenching even. I have to confess tears were involved...more than once. Both books together make a really good complete picture and both have their right to exist next to each other.<br><br>All in all, an enjoyable read and from what I've seen so far, Ms. Sheridan is an author to check out.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447539995i/17017465.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1758614995" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1758614995" />
    <a title="Chantal ❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39644830-chantal"><img alt="Chantal ❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491092006p2/39644830.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1758614995?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chantal ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chantal ❤️" href="/user/show/39644830-chantal">Chantal ❤️</a>

          marked it as read-when-i-am-brainless

<div id="review_771926544" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/771926544" />
    <a title="Alba and Her Secrets..♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets"><img alt="Alba and Her Secrets..♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410338915p2/15917463.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/771926544?book_show_action=true">Nov 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alba and Her Secrets..♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alba and Her Secrets..♥" href="/user/show/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets">Alba and Her Secrets..♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=holy-hotness">holy-hotness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=6-stars">6-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=abuse-mental-issues">abuse-mental-issues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=favorite-author">favorite-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=best-hero">best-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=draaaaama">draaaaama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15917463-alba-and-her-secrets?shelf=tattooed-pierced">tattooed-pierced</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer771926544" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15397944303419043002"><b>5+ "I choose you" Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s196.photobucket.com/user/Albyz92/media/Collages%20Goodreads/Leo%20-%20Mia%20Sheridan_zps7ozceduu.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450375580i/17417845.png' alt=' photo Leo - Mia Sheridan_zps7ozceduu.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>After a quite bad read I needed a feel good and sweet novel and I knew Mia Sheridan would be a good choice. Earlier this year I read my first book by her (<i>Archer's Voice</i>) and I loved it so I decided to give it another try and now read <i>Leo</i> (which happens to be Sheridan's debut novel). <br/><br/>First let me say this in advance, I believe I will not be able to review this book without 'spoilering' something. The whole book and one of the characters in particular has this secret a</span>
  <span id="freeText15397944303419043002" style="display:none"><b>5+ "I choose you" Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s196.photobucket.com/user/Albyz92/media/Collages%20Goodreads/Leo%20-%20Mia%20Sheridan_zps7ozceduu.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450375580i/17417845.png" alt=" photo Leo - Mia Sheridan_zps7ozceduu.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After a quite bad read I needed a feel good and sweet novel and I knew Mia Sheridan would be a good choice. Earlier this year I read my first book by her (<i>Archer's Voice</i>) and I loved it so I decided to give it another try and now read <i>Leo</i> (which happens to be Sheridan's debut novel). <br><br>First let me say this in advance, I believe I will not be able to review this book without 'spoilering' something. The whole book and one of the characters in particular has this secret and it happens to be everywhere in this book. I literally read 10% of Leo and I already suspected on the 'big secret' so PLEASE if you haven't read this book and you want to, DO NOT CONTINUE READING my review. You've been warned ;)<br><br><i>Leo</i> is a stand-alone (that belongs to Sheridan's <i>A Sign of Love</i> novels) and it tells the story of two kids that have grown up together in foster care: these are Leo McKenna and Evelyn "Evie" Cruise. They start as friends (Evie being 10 and Leo 11) and obviously, as time passes, they fall in love. However, Leo is adopted at the age of 15 and has to leave his beloved's side. He promises he will come back for her...<br><br><i>
  <b>"I'm going to kiss you now, Evie, and when I do, it's going to mean that you're mine. I don't care how far away from each other we are. You. Are. Mine. I'll wait for you. And I want you to wait for me. Promise me you won't let anyone else touch you. Promise me you'll save yourself for me."</b>
</i><br><br>And he never came back. We do not know why and with that eight years pass. Now, Evie is 22, she is free and she is living a decent life (even though, she had quite a difficult past thanks to her druggie mother). She works, she can pay a little apartment for her and she has amazing friends (loved Nicole and Landon to pieces!!). However, her love life is nule after having her heart broken by the love of her life. <br><br>Then.. Jake Madsen a.k.a "creepy stalker" appears. He is rich, super handsome and he is kind of stalking Evie (who happens to enjoy it a little bit!!). After some time they actually talk and Jake comes with news about Leo. News that Evie was not expecting after eight years.. Also, the news that Evie happens to be very VERY attracked to Jake, of course!<br><br><i>
  <b>"You know, I'm sure there are girls all over the city who would love the opportunity to be stalked by you. It really doesn't seem fair that you focus all your creepiness on me."<br>He smiles. "I've decided I like focusing on you, though, Evie."</b>
</i><br><br>They feel a very strong connection towards each other and they start dating. Evie and Jake are the sweetest and hottest together. I love Mia Sheridan's characters and the ones in <i>Leo</i> were not an exception. So, Jake and Evie are dating and they feel this connection which reminds me so much of the one she had with Leo.. Evie senses that as well and she also sees that Jake is hiding something.<br><br><i>
  <b>He rips his mouth from mine as he growls, "Mine. Only mine. Only. Ever. Mine," still slamming into me, pounding me against the wall.<br><br>I had made a promise a long time ago and although that person was no longer a part of my life, nor was he ever going to be, somewhere inside I always knew that if I was going to fall in love again, it was going to be because something in that man reminded me of Leo.</b>
</i><br><br>The novel is a mix of Evie's present and flashbacks and well.. Obviously, there is quite a surprise towards the ending: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I mean, it was obivious to me that Jake was Leo. Their connection and the hiding, it was quite clear to me. . <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I very much suspected of it since the beggining but still I really enjoyed Leo. I enjoyed it so much. <br><br><i>
  <b>"I love you, Evie," he says quietly. "Whatever you think about what I'm about to tell you, you have to know that. I've always loved you. I've never stopped. Not for one second in eight years."</b>
</i><br><br>I loved the writing. The main and secondary characters. And specially the chemistry between the couple. As always, Sheridan does not fail on that! And the ending! Awwwwww, it was just so freaking sweet! I love cheesy, lovey dovey, love you forever kind of ending haha ;)<br><br><i>
  <b>Everyone tells a story about themselves in their own head. That story makes you what you are, dictating all your actions and all your mistakes. If your own story is filled with guilt and fear and self-hatred, life can look pretty miserable.<br>But, if you're very lucky, you might have a person who tells you a better story, one that takes up residence in your soul, speaking louder than the woeful tale you've convinced yourself of. If you let it speak loudly within your heart, it becomes your passion and your purpose. And this is a good thing, the best of things. Because it is the very definition of love, nothing less.</b>
</i><br><br>Therefore, my rating is (clearly) 6 STARS because I simply loved this novel: just the whole thing (writing, characters, plot, etc.). I think it was an amazing debut book and I cannot wait to read the other ones written by Mia Sheridan. So, if you haven't read anything by her or you haven't read <i>Leo</i>, please do, I highly recommend it! :)<br><br><b>CHECK OUT MY BLOG HERE:</b><br><a href="http://albaandhersecrets.blog.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447323775i/16986965.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1503264943" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1503264943" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1503264943?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=tragedy-mystery-love-hope">tragedy-mystery-love-hope</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=love-drama">love-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=bad-ending">bad-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=hero-turns-out-to-be-a-jackass">hero-turns-out-to-be-a-jackass</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1503264943" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12278128166242479354">I finished reading this book in one day and it was going to be one of my favorite books with “5 stars” but it lost me in the last 20 percent after “the twist of the story”.<br/><br/>I was left so disappointed that it felt as if someone had taken something I loved dearly from me. I really would rather it had evolved into something else.<br/><br/>***********************************************<br/><br/>“LEO” is the story of two kids from a foster care who love each other very much and it is really an emotional book. The story </span>
  <span id="freeText12278128166242479354" style="display:none">I finished reading this book in one day and it was going to be one of my favorite books with “5 stars” but it lost me in the last 20 percent after “the twist of the story”.<br><br>I was left so disappointed that it felt as if someone had taken something I loved dearly from me. I really would rather it had evolved into something else.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br>“LEO” is the story of two kids from a foster care who love each other very much and it is really an emotional book. The story touched me from the very beginning, but even during the happiest moments, there was a lump in my throat as to what was going to be revealed that would make me unhappy because there were signs of something disturbing to come, something sad. <br><br>I knew it all along but I couldn’t put my finger on what it was. Actually, I had two theories as to what it was, both turning out to be wrong in the end :( <br><br>***********************************************<br><br>When I read the twist of the story, I was shocked because I did not see it coming. Up until the “twist”, I was happy – I was saying, “Well everyone has secrets. So what? He will explain it in the end and she will understand...” <br><br>She did, but I did not! When the full truth was revealed, I was saying to myself “Oh... WTF?” with resentment and frustration. I did not expect it at all. I did not expect to be so disappointed in the hero. <br><br>I still have difficulty in understanding and forgiving – maybe it is because forgiving is not one of my strong suits. I wanted to throw away my kindle or hit the hero with it at that point!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1475691087ra/20752788.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Here is why I was so disappointed: <br><br>BIG SPOILERS HERE, BE CAREFUL!<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>Leo left Evie to go and live with his new foster parents and made a promise to her to keep in touch. He said he would always love her and would come back for her when she was 18. He told her to wait for him. He says these words:<br><br> <i>“I'm going to kiss you now, Evie, and when I do, it's going to mean that you're mine. I don't care how far away from each other we are. You. Are. Mine. I'll wait for you. And I want you to wait for me. Promise me you won't let anyone else touch you. Promise me you'll save yourself for me.” </i><br>And then what? <br><br>After 3 days in his new home, he let his so-called new mum fuck him!!!! <br>He felt so guilty that he could not find himself worthy of Evie any more and that is why, he never contacted her. No calls, no letters! Zero, zilch, zip, nada, nothing!!!<br><br>She was so sad, so desperate and she never knew what happened to her LEO.<br><br>And let’s go back to our dear Leo, he felt so guilty that he let it go on for years and years. <br><br>He felt so guilty that he used drugs and messed with as many women as possible to piss the mother!<br>OK, let me try to be more understanding. He was young and this may be considered a case of pedophilia, but well, the “pedophile” here was a woman and he was a guy at the age of 14. <br><br>Why, why on earth didn't he say no? <br>Was a gun pointed at him? <br>Was she stronger than him? <br>NOOOO !<br><br>His explanation of being easily seduced by his mother was being a young horny boy who drank 2 shots, which made me hate the hero all of a sudden. <br><br>While explaining his reasons, Leo also said that he let it go on for so long and did not confess it to his father because he was happy with what the family offered him - the house, the luxuries etc. <br><br>Yuck ! I hated him for that, too...<br><br>Well, Evie has forgiven him easily, but I cannot... I am also pissed that she can forgive him without enough groveling! (Well, no groveling would be enough for me to forgive Leo, though).<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>And here I say to the writer, “Why did you make Leo do all that ?– it just does not fit the character at all. After a few days of their separation, while he was missing her that much (we learn it later from his beautiful letters), how can you make him do it? <br><br>I just don’t understand and I think I will put the blame on the writer rather than the hero himself. Well, maybe, the book deserves 5 points with all this beautiful story telling, the deep emotions and the hot chemistry between them which was felt on every page, in every sentence, but I am so angry with the writer for ruining such a beautiful love story for me; hence my low grade.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br>And here is one more thing that made me question the book... This is the most important revelation - please don't read if you have not read the book and intend to read it.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>I said that I did not expect Jake would turn out to be Leo because I really did not think Evie would not recognize him. He might have changed in 8 years growing up from being a teenager to an adult and the surgeries etc but a person's voice hardly changes and his eyes, for God's sake, can't have changed. How on earth can't she understand that Jake is her Leo?<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> That was totally unconvincing...<br><br>If you ask me, this book is a waste of time with this ending... It is very frustrating!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="12278128166242479354" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
