<div id="review_559265319" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559265319" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559265319?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17608346-leo">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559265319" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12756387730494076871"><b>4 1/2 Rooftop Stars!</b><br/> <br/><b>
  <i>"This is not goodbye, Evie. Remember our promise. Don't ever forget our promise. I will come back for you.”~ Leo</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413112i/812993.jpg' width='340' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I really enjoyed Mia Sheridan’s writing in her debut novel Leo! I loved the characters and the past/present presentation of the story line. I found myself engrossed in the story from the prologue. <br/> <br/>Leo is the story of Evie and Leo two foster children who have survived horrible upbringings and have found home in each other. Through the years they fall in love. </span>
  <span id="freeText12756387730494076871" style="display:none"><b>4 1/2 Rooftop Stars!</b><br> <br><b>
  <i>"This is not goodbye, Evie. Remember our promise. Don't ever forget our promise. I will come back for you.”~ Leo</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413112i/812993.jpg" width="340" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I really enjoyed Mia Sheridan’s writing in her debut novel Leo! I loved the characters and the past/present presentation of the story line. I found myself engrossed in the story from the prologue. <br> <br>Leo is the story of Evie and Leo two foster children who have survived horrible upbringings and have found home in each other. Through the years they fall in love. I found that their teenage love story was just beautiful and I just loved the prologue. <br><br><b>
  <i>”Maybe I’m an open book, or maybe love is like a magnifying glass straight into the souls of those who own your heart.”~Evie</i>
</b><br><br>When Leo gets adopted and has to move across the country, he makes some big promises and declarations to Evie. <br><br><b>
  <i>”Then before we know it, you’ll be 18 and I’ll be able to come back for you. We’ll make a life together.”~ Leo</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”It will only ever be you, Evie.”</i>
</b><br><br>Sadly eight years have come and gone and Evie never hears from Leo. She has made a safe life for herself on her own and has accumulated some wonderful friends. She works hard for all that she has. She is a beautiful, witty, caring and wonderful person. Despite the hand she has been dealt in this world, she is the kind of person a friend would value. <br> <br>Evie realizes that she is being followed by a handsome stranger and is shocked to find out that he is sent on behalf of Leo to check in on her. Jake delivers some crushing news and slowly Evie and Jake start spending time together. Jake seems to have some secrets, he is rather vague about his past and there are one or two woman who seem to be circling around him. <br><br>Jake Madsen and Evie fall in love but this story takes a couple of twists and turns and through love, salvation and a happily ever after, this reader was left with a smile on her face.<br><br>The only aspect of this book that didn’t work for me was the cover. I felt that this kind of story deemed something different than the promise of sex as the cover offers. <br><br><b>
  <i>”All the world’s a circus. Sometimes you choose your act and sometimes it’s assigned to you. I had roamed the arena for far too long, roaring and bellowing, believing that I wasn’t brave enough to leap through fire. But all along, she had stood there, constant and calm.”</i>
</b><br><br>Beautiful story job well done Mia Sheridan!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12756387730494076871" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1562894423" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1562894423" />
    <a title="Rose" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22312397-rose"><img alt="Rose" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601368419p2/22312397.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1562894423?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rose" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rose" href="/user/show/22312397-rose">Rose</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1562894423" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11118732500019937331">A lot, A LOT of things didn't work out for me in this one... I'm kinda shocked it's the same author that wrote Archer's voice and Kyland.... Extremely long rant ahead.<br/><br/>2 Stars: <br/><br/>I liked this book for the most part, I really did.. but the TWIST, the reason why he left her for 8 years and never spoke to her, DID NOT JUSTIFY ANYTHING. I was pissed. <br/><br/><b> IF I READ ANOTHER BOOK WHERE THE HEROINE IS COMPLETELY CELIBATE DURING A SEPARATION AND THE HERO LITERALLY WHORES AROUND, I WILL LITERALLY THROW MY KINDL</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11118732500019937331" style="display:none">A lot, A LOT of things didn't work out for me in this one... I'm kinda shocked it's the same author that wrote Archer's voice and Kyland.... Extremely long rant ahead.<br /><br />2 Stars: <br /><br />I liked this book for the most part, I really did.. but the TWIST, the reason why he left her for 8 years and never spoke to her, DID NOT JUSTIFY ANYTHING. I was pissed. <br /><br /><b> IF I READ ANOTHER BOOK WHERE THE HEROINE IS COMPLETELY CELIBATE DURING A SEPARATION AND THE HERO LITERALLY WHORES AROUND, I WILL LITERALLY THROW MY KINDLE OUT OF MY WINDOW (ok not literally, but I think you guys understand my anger </b> <br /><br />Okay, let's start about what this is about. It starts quite beautifully as per usual with Mia Sheridan (whose books I LOVED previously). A young Evie and Leo meet throughout foster care. When Leo is 15, and Evie is 14, Leo is being adopted into a family, and he asks her to wait for him: <br /><br /><b> <i> I'm going to kiss you now Evie, and when I do, it's going to mean that you're mine. I don't care how far away from each other we are. You. Are. Mine. I'll wait for you. And I want you to wait for me. Promise me you won't let anyone else touch you. Promise me you'll save yourself for me, and only me. </i></b>  <br /><br />Fast forward 8 years, Evie hasn't heard from Leo once. Then, she meets a stranger, Jake, a guy who tells her Leo sent him to make sure Evie is okay. And from there, their romance begins. <br /><br />Now, this 'romance', was WAY too unbelievable! She was celibate for 8 years as promised to Leo, hasn't done other sexual things as well, and by the second date, she immediately sleeps with Jake. Really, I mean you wait until you're 22 and you immediately sleep with Jake? I found that unbelievable. <br /><br />Also, before she properly meets Jake, she knows he's been following her around, like a stalker. Now, I know it's fiction, but some reality is needed! As oppose to being freaked the hell out (specially cause the lock on her front gate is broken), she smiles when she sees him and is sad when he's not following her. Umm? That is not a normal reaction. But okay, whatever. They fall in love in like 2.5 seconds<br /><br />Back to Jake and Evie. I felt like Jake's characterisation was badly done. I'm sorry to say this, but I feel like the author knows the hype about 'alpha-men' and how much us readers love them (me included), but Jake's alpha-ness was extremely unconvincing and it contrasted COMPLETELY to the other side of him, the sensitive loving one, that it ended up being completely unbelievable. He goes all Christian Grey on her with his demands, and her submission (where she always does as he says). I'm sorry to say, but I think this would have been A LOT better if the author stuck to creating a sweet, protective guy, and not Christian Grey wanna-be, with the hold "Now, finish your food." It was just so random in the story and creeped me out because I felt like that wasn't really him. I LOVE alphas, they're my favourite heroes, but it DID NOT work here at all. <br /><br />Then there's Evie. While I admired how genuinely sweet she was, it was too good to be true. Considering her past experiences, I expected someone realistically more critical about trusting someone so quickly and letting them in. Also, I think the author imitated the whole 50 shades thing where he commands things and she agrees. She was quite the pushover at times and it pissed me off. When she catches his lies 3 or 4 times, he NEVER justifies because 'he's not ready', and he just says 'just trust me'. And she says yes. Umm, lady, you saw him with different women at different times, don't you think you need an explanation? It was kind of pathetic to hear her say "but I trust him, so it's okay." No women! Get an explanation! Throughout the whole book, he doesn't offer ANY explanation despite his EXTREMELY DODGY AND SKETCHY ACTIONS. <br /><br />Then, of course, there's the extreme predictability of the story. As in, I'm sorry, we kinda all know that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Jake was Leo, if he was the love of her life, how the hell does she not recognise him? Hell, I recognised my grade 2 teacher (I was a lot younger than 15 then) when I was 19. I mean... really? You were 14 not 2  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />Oh and alas, the twist! Spoilers ahead about the twist, for those of you who wanna give it a shot and wanna hear why I chose to give this 2 stars and not 4, without reading specifics, essentially it's this: throughout the separation, she's celibate, he's a manwhore, and his justification DID NOT CUT IT FOR ME. I considered it cheating. <br /><br /><b> I will never condone a book where the hero is a manwhore during a separation and the heroine is celibate. Unless 1- The heroine did something HORRIBLE to the hero like broke his heart and he believed she didn't want him, or 2 - If the hero thought she was dead. </b> <br /><br />Now here's the thing, reading Mia Sheridan's stories before and knowing how POWERFUL the love was and faithful the characters are, I was actually 100% sure it would be the latter, that Leo thought Evie was dead which is why he had so many women after, but of course not... the hero had to be a douche. The spoiler will go into specifics: <br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Okay folks, now, read my first quote. He promises Evie to wait for her, and to send her letters immediately, and three days later, THREE DAYS LATER, he has sex with his step-mom. It's basically the same EXACT situation as Mrs.Robinson in 50 shades of grey. Now here's the thing, when he began saying the story, my heart was breaking because I thought it was going to get into sexual assault, but here's the thing, Leo never said no... The step-mom is an effed up pedophile, but he never said no. Even years after, he never said no, and in fact, when HE FINALLY DID SAY NO TO HER, she didn't force him. There was one scene in the hospital where my heart broke for him when she didn't take no for an answer, but that was the only time it was forced. Three days after promising himself to Evie, he has sex with his step-mom. Now my issues (a bit descriptive, sorry) Why did he agree to drink with her and play pool with her while drinking? But okay, let's say that was just cause he was a kid. But then, she didn't even go on top of him or so, he says he was a horny kid who had two shots, and then she: <br /><br /><b> <i> Finally, she just got completely naked and bent over the pool table and started begging me to take her. She seduced me, but I didn't resist very fervently. </i></b> . So he made the decision to go to her and have sex with her. <br /><br />Afterwards, he HATES himself, justifiably so, I hated him. I expected him to say "no!" And remember his love for Evie, the girl he promised his life to. And despite hating himself over it, does he stop? Nope. He goes deep into self-hatred. <br /><br /><b> <i> I had promised you I would save myself for you, be true to you, and it took less than a week for me to betray you. </i></b>  <br /><br />Did she take advantage of him? ABSOLUTELY. SHE DESERVED TO GO TO JAIL, and I hated that no retribution came to her, but anyways, he always consented. He even awknoledged that he could have done more than he did to stop it... And if he truly loved Evie, his hatred should have made him stop after that first time, but of course not, heroes nowadays have to be ASSHOLES. He says: <b> <i> it happened regularly until the day I moved out and went to college </i></b> . This is where the step mom tries to continue things, but he says no, and she actually takes it as a no and leaves. SO WHY COULDN'T HE HAVE SAID NO BEFORE? <br /><br />And then, why he continues not reaching out to Evie? Of course, the hero feels broken, so as oppose to fighting for the love of his life AFTER HE FINALLY GETS AWAY FROM THE CLUTCHES OF HIS NASTY STEP-MOM, he thinks she's too good for him. <br /><br /><b> <i> I started drinking, doing drugs, partying, using girls. </i></b>  He did this because he despised himself for doing what he did to Evie, as oppose to fixing it, he has sex with like a million girls. <br /><br />Anyways, after all the women, he gets in a massive car accident, "a part of him dies and is reborn" and he realises he wants Evie again. <br /><br />And here, after Evie is being a pushover throughout the whole book and allowing him not justify the myriad of women that answer his phone / he's with, etc, she is WAY too forgiving. In fact, when she finds out he's Leo, he's been lying this WHOLE TIME. She has sex with him almost immediately when she sees him for the talk. Umm, I would have been DEVASTATED. <br /><br />Do I believe he loved her? Yes, I do. I just think sometimes that's not enough. I loved his tattoo, I liked that Gwen (an ex-lover) told her "you'll never be her, he'll try to shape you into her" or something like that, which proves that he always had Evie in his mind, but I needed him to freaking GROVEL, and I'm talking about MONTHS. The letters in the end were cute, but I can't get over that one day after writing this: <br /><br /><b> <i> You already know I'm going to marry you someday and so it's okay if you know the place I want to ask you. I'll try to keep the ring and the words I plan to say to you under wraps. haha. I love you Evie. I'll love you forever. Your leo </i></b>  He has sex with his step-mom. <br /><br />I don't know if I would've forgiven him for ALL the girls considering she waited for him completely. <br /><br />OH AND the thing that PISSED ME OFF, when he tries to explain a part of why he didn't stop with the step-mom: <br /><br /><b> <i> I loved the stuff they were giving me; the luxuries, the trips, stuff I never had before. And that made me hate myself the most. </i></b> . So, are we supposed to forgive him for doing one girl after the other, while ignoring Evie, because HE FELT SO BAD. He also claims that he suffered as much as Evie. Umm, no you didn't. She's working 2 jobs and has hardly a social life and you broke her heart. <br /><br />Anyways, in the END, she forgives him WAY too easily. Man, for as much as Evie loved Leo, I would have been destroyed at his inability to remain faithful.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Also, can I add things that I didn't like as a whole: <br /><br />1. She didn't recognise leo, already mentioned that.<br />2. She never saw the tattoo on his back? Dude, IT'S MASSIVE and you guys have had sex like a million times. <br />3. She's a virgin till 22 and has sex with him on a second date, bam bam thank you mam. <br />4. Their falling in love was too quick and a bit unbelievable<br />5. Too 50 shades for my liking<br />6. Too cliche / predictable<br />7. Her heart breaks for him when he tells her about the women and how broken he is. Umm, I would be furious but ok. <br />7. When she finds out he's Leo, I expected him to be KISSING HER FEET from regret, but this is what happens when she sees him again: <br /><b> <i> He closes his eyes for a minute like he's really just too tired to deal with my attitude </i></b>  Umm, I'm sorry, is her attitude (which is completely pliant anyways) too much for you considering she thought you were dead / now knows you've effed a million women despite your promise to her? <br /><br />Then: <br /><br /><b> <i> He sighs as if he's barely tolerating me. "Sit down Evie. Now." </i></b>  Man, if this is how someone spoke to me when they BETRAYED ME, I'd go mental, but of course she listens to him like she did the entire book. <br /><br />Okay, I think rant done. <br /><br />Oh, one last thing. I was EXTREMELY disappointed in the author for a part where Evie asks Jake if he's been with a lot of women, and he says there have been MANY but he hasn't dated any. That Evie's different. Okay, I like manwhores, but THEN when he asks her if she's dated a lot, she says there's been many but no one serious (as a joke) and he's furious about it. Then when she says the truth to him, that there hasn't been anyone, he says "because you're a better person than me". Sex partners does not tell you how good a person is or not. <br /><br />Okay, NOW i think my rant is done. I used to purchase Mia sheridan's books on spot, cause I loved all her previous ones, but now, I learnt I need to be cautious. <br /><br />Take into considering I'm a VERY minor opinion. You could like it if you're more forgiving than me. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11118732500019937331" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Promise me you'll save yourself for me."</b> ~Leo<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br><br><b>"He came to say goodbye to me the night before he left and he kissed me for the very first time. And when I say he kissed me, I mean it was like a vow, that kiss. I've heard people say they lose themselves in a kiss, but it was like we found ourselves the second our lips met. It was like he took me apart and put me back together with that kiss."</b> ~Evie<br><br>Evie and Leo meet in foster care, they become best friends and fall in love. The day Leo finds out he is being adopted and moving clear across the country is the day everything in Evie's life changes. Because the boy who promised to love her, stay in touch with her and eventually comeback for her never does ...<br><br><b>"I knew Leo. He asked me to check on you."</b> ~Jake<br><br>Eight years later Evie is being stalked by a guy who claims to be sent by Leo. Jake. Evie and Jake are connected in more ways then Evie can imagine. Jake is hiding something though. Something that has haunted him for years. <br><br><i>
  <b>'He's also leaving something out. I don't know exactly how I know this, I just do.'</b>
</i> ~ Inner monologue of Evie<br><br>Evie can sense that he is withholding something; yet the intense pull she feels toward Jake has her falling in love with him regardless of his secrets.<br><br><br>When the truth is revealed will Evie stand by Jake?<br><br>Is love enough?<br><br><br><b>FAVORITES</b><br><br><u>Fave things unsaid...</u><br><br>'And when he laughs like that, I swear a piece of my soul, the part of me that keeps secrets even from myself, tries to lunge towards him, like his happiness is an invisible pull to my own heart. It's crazy. I don't even know this guy.' ~Evie<br><br><br><u>Heart stopping lines...</u><br><br><b>"And, Evie, when you walk away from people, even strangers, you gotta know that their eyes follow you. And I'll tell you why because I've felt it myself. It's because they don't want to see the light that is Evie, the light that is you, walking away from them. They want to see it coming towards them and staying with them."</b> ~Jake<br><br><b>"God, Evie,"</b> he whispers.<b> "You feel so good. You smell so good. You undo me. And I haven't even had you yet. What will that do to me?"</b><br>~Jake<br><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>This story griped me from the first page, I loved it!! I recommend this to all New Adult book lovers!!!<br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Lovable<br>Writing Style- Good, has a unique twist<br>Plot/Storyline- Captured my intention from the first page and never let go<br>Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br>Overall- I loved it!!! READ IT!!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6185159470365290905">4.5<br/><br/><b>"Why are you looking at me?" <br/> "Because I like your face."</b><br/><br/>In Leo, Mia Sheridan does it again. She brings romance, heart, grit, and tenderness to every story that she creates. I found myself swept away by this beautiful piece.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433127045i/15053669.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Leo begins in the past. We meet Evie and Leo. Both wards of the state, they have found friendship, acceptance, and love in each other. Both having to endure the hardships of the foster system, they find solace in each other.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433127045i/15053671.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/> <b>"Maybe I'm an open book, or maybe love is like a</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6185159470365290905" style="display:none">4.5<br><br><b>"Why are you looking at me?" <br> "Because I like your face."</b><br><br>In Leo, Mia Sheridan does it again. She brings romance, heart, grit, and tenderness to every story that she creates. I found myself swept away by this beautiful piece.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433127045i/15053669.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Leo begins in the past. We meet Evie and Leo. Both wards of the state, they have found friendship, acceptance, and love in each other. Both having to endure the hardships of the foster system, they find solace in each other.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433127045i/15053671.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>"Maybe I'm an open book, or maybe love is like a magnifying glass straight into the souls of those who own your heart."</b><br><br>When Leo is fifteen, he is forced to say goodbye to Evie. He has been adopted and is moving away. He vows to find her when she is 18. They share a tender moment on the roof under a blanket of snow.<br><br> <b>"I don't ever want to stop looking at him. I don't ever want to stop being near him. But he's moving across the country, and there's nothing we can do."-Evie</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433127045i/15053672._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>8 years later....</b><br><br> Evie is alone. She is making a way working as a maid. She is living a simple life. She enjoys reading and spending time with her friends. Only one thing is missing in her life....Leo!<br>She recognizes a stranger following her. <br><br> <b>"Someone is following me. He's been doing it for a week and a half now. He's crap at it. I marked him almost immediately and I've been watching him as he's been watching me. Clearly, he's no professional. But I can't think of one single reason why someone is following me around town."-Evie</b><br><br>The stalker turns out to be a friend of Leo's named Jake. Jake is everything Evie is not. He is a polished business man with plenty of money, polish, and class. He is drawn to her. She is drawn to him. Although Evie doesn't have much experience with men, she begins to spend time with Jake. <br><br>Jake is a bit of a mystery. There are several instances where she fears he is lying to her. Evie is especially sensitive because of the numerous differences between the two. He is educated and running a multi million dollar company. Evie has her GED and is working as a maid. Every time Evie hesitates with Jake, he draws her back in.<br><br> <b>"Please, just trust me, please don't go."-Jake</b><br><br><b>"I follow Jake and my heart once again. But hoping deep inside, that that doesn’t make me a fool."-Evie</b><br><br>Their relationship soon transforms into a passionate love affair. Jake and Evie find connection on every level. This is a tender friends to lovers story. <br><br><b>"He takes the back of my head in his hand and tilts it so that he can plunge his tongue in deep, and then we're kissing like we can't get enough of each other, like if a herd of zebras trampled through his living room right now, we wouldn't even come up for air."-Evie</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433127045i/15053673.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall, Leo was a beautiful read. All of the quesitons are answered. I won't lie, I private messaged a friend with several questions along the way. In true Sheridan fashion, she has crafted a story that will stay with me forever. I can recommend with out hesitancy this read to anyone that enjoys a tender romance and a story of broken things made beautiful. There was a high level of angst as you try to put the pieces together. Still, it was an unforgettable read! Days later I am still thinking about it. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432876482ra/15015417.gif" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </span>

<div id="review_593569589" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/593569589" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/593569589?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer593569589" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15589135281820293134"><b>3 Stars</b><br/><br/>This sweet and touching story greatly showcases the power of love and the unsurpassable beauty of <b>redemption</b>. It opens with an emotional glimpse into the childhood of these broken characters, and quickly unites with present time-- sprinkling in important flashbacks as the story progresses. <br/><br/><b>Evie</b> has come a long way from the lost and neglected little girl she once was. But one thing remains constant--her undying longing for her childhood best friend and first love--Leo. Although she has acc</span>
  <span id="freeText15589135281820293134" style="display:none"><b>3 Stars</b><br><br>This sweet and touching story greatly showcases the power of love and the unsurpassable beauty of <b>redemption</b>. It opens with an emotional glimpse into the childhood of these broken characters, and quickly unites with present time-- sprinkling in important flashbacks as the story progresses. <br><br><b>Evie</b> has come a long way from the lost and neglected little girl she once was. But one thing remains constant--her undying longing for her childhood best friend and first love--Leo. Although she has accepted his disappearance and his broken promises, she continues to quietly save her heart for the boy who broke it all those years ago...<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I'm going to kiss you now, Evie, and when I do, it's going to mean that you're mine.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>When <b>Jake</b> stalks into Evie's life, armed with determination and information on Leo, Evie's world seems to finally come alive again. He sparks things inside her that she's never felt, but he also harbors secrets that could ultimately break the solid ground she now stands upon.<br><br>I really enjoyed the way this story progressed, and how we were gradually introduced to its secrets. The twist in the plot was easy to decipher, but I got the feeling that we were <i>purposely</i> being clued in ahead of time. As if the shock value of this story was meant for the characters and not necessarily the readers—allowing us the suspense of watching the truths unfold. <br><br>Jake was a passionate, bossy, and sexy hero. There were some areas of his character that lacked a little depth, but his guarded persona was warranted. The steamy scenes intense and descriptively sensual.<br><br>Evie—hands down—MADE this story, for me! Her <i>actions</i> built her character, not her inner dialogue, which was a true testament to this author's amazing execution. Instead of wallowing in the <i>why me's</i>, Evie uses her tortured childhood as motivation to rise above. The world has given her so many reasons to never trust it again--but she does. Heartache, neglect, poverty, and instability has plagued the precious years of her youth-- but she <b>perseveres</b>. Not only is she an inspirational heroine, but an amazing example of how every negative in life can be used to gain a positive perspective. Evie, and all that she represents, became the heart and soul of this book. <b>Very sweet read!</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Why are you looking at me?"<br>"Because I like your face."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Romance/NA<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Extremely steamy<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Slow burn, intense, adorable. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Broken and garded. Sexy, bossy hero. Lovable heroine. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Unique execution. Twist in plot. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Engaging. <br><b>▪ POV:</b> 1st Person: Heroine<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> POV switch<br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1482167868" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1482167868" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1482167868?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1482167868" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3745289445615218585">This is a pretty good story of friends to lovers, second chance kind of love between two children who met in foster care. One gets adopted, one gets left behind but they promise to find each other when they are eighteen. ~Sigh~ Of course, <i>that</i> doesn't happen. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451374993i/17535221.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have a lot of conflicting feelings about this story. I was intrigued and couldn't put the book down but it was blatantly obvious who a certain person was. Fortunately, there are enough twists that it keeps you on your toes and keeps you </span>
  <span id="freeText3745289445615218585" style="display:none">This is a pretty good story of friends to lovers, second chance kind of love between two children who met in foster care. One gets adopted, one gets left behind but they promise to find each other when they are eighteen. ~Sigh~ Of course, <i>that</i> doesn't happen. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451374993i/17535221.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have a lot of conflicting feelings about this story. I was intrigued and couldn't put the book down but it was blatantly obvious who a certain person was. Fortunately, there are enough twists that it keeps you on your toes and keeps you interested...well, at least it did for me. <br><br>Both Leo and Evie are quite enjoyable and you just can't help but pull for them especially with all they've been through. And they're just so sweet in that first puppy love kind of way. <br><br>Fast forward eight years and Evie has someone following her. Turns out it's a friend of Leo's named Jake who was sent to check in on Evie. Things progress quite quickly but there are things about Jake that just don't add up and slowly but surely, things come to light. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1451374993ra/17535224.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jake and Evie were quite a lovely couple as well but their relationship was also a bit disconcerting. What Jake did was not right but Evie should've taken time <i>then</i> to figure out things and really look at the signs. <br><br>There's drama and there's angst but finally we get some answers and it's as bad as we thought it would be. Luckily, Evie has a great support system and is able to get to her true feelings. <br><br>I thought things got resolved a bit too quickly but overall I was happy with the story and the epilogue was really sweet. <br><br>There's a second book from Leo's POV called <i>Leo's Chance</i>. Hopefully, it's not a total rehash of the same story and we get some good insights. <i>(ETA: It is a rehash but there are plenty of new things to keep things moving along. But more than that...the ending and extra epilogues make it highly worth reading!)</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451374993i/17535225.jpg" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quote:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ "I can remain steady and strong, because I believe in you. Because you are mine."</span>
  <a data-text-id="3745289445615218585" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1823381096" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1823381096" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1823381096" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5661316694022957733">Leo is the debut novel by one of my favourite authors, Mia Sheridan. I've read a few that she has written after this one, which I have really liked, but this one...let me just add that I am in the minority here...didn't work for me. It failed to excite me.......<blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480289329ra/21293378.gif' alt=' photo raw_zpsx4yqhttj.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote>I'm going to try and keep my "rant" as short as possible.<br/><br/>The writing was nothing like the other books...it was just okay. No great quotes stood out to me!!!<br/><br/>There were so many things that glaringly reminded me of 50 Shades of G</span>
  <span id="freeText5661316694022957733" style="display:none">Leo is the debut novel by one of my favourite authors, Mia Sheridan. I've read a few that she has written after this one, which I have really liked, but this one...let me just add that I am in the minority here...didn't work for me. It failed to excite me.......<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480289329ra/21293378.gif" alt=" photo raw_zpsx4yqhttj.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>I'm going to try and keep my "rant" as short as possible.<br><br>The writing was nothing like the other books...it was just okay. No great quotes stood out to me!!!<br><br>There were so many things that glaringly reminded me of 50 Shades of Grey.....all that internal dialogue, the broken and dominant hero, the sweet and virginal heroine, etc, etc<br><br>So, the heroine is still at a virgin....she promised to wait for Leo, remember.......and then..........presto.............2 dates and she sleeps with the hero...who is not Leo!!!!<br><br>Can I do some eye exercises here please!!!!!<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480289329ra/21293379.gif" alt=" photo housewives-roll_zpszklwjmzq.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>I actually liked Evie, the heroine. She was a really sweet and likeable characters......but when she starts telling her besties and friends all of Leo's secrets and how much she loves him....blah blah..........I just couldn't believable that any sane person who do that, even if it's her very best best BFF...............<br><br>I couldn't engage with Jake, the hero.........his whole attitude was ...ooh I'm so great.........and quite honestly, I can't believe a guy that age would be running a company like he does!!! Oh, did you say he's like Mr Christian Grey????? Really!!! Guess there's a lot of hot hot very very rich very very young zillionaires out there that I am not aware of!!!Or not!!! Ummm<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480289329ra/21293380.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_njo81xucYY1skolcto1_500_zps83qqxj2c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Yes, some more eye exercises after this......<br><br>Evie sleeps with Jake....lots and lots and lots of times and she never never ever sees the ginormous tattoo on his back.........what, they just do the missionary position in the dark!!!! Seriously!!! And to test my intelligence further....Evie DOES NOT recognize Leo when she sees him after all those many years........come one...<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[so, he's had plastic surgery but still, I found this part very hard to swallow....... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480289844ra/21293410.gif" alt=" photo Hermione_eye_roll_zps1vndilfg.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>So when Evie discovers Jake's big secret - she's heartbroken for him...naturally!!! She's a sweet and loving and caring person.......and she's totally so understanding......really!!! The guy has slept his way through the years.....she's remained a virgin.........allright, so I can't exactly expect a person to keep their virginity in this day and age......but why can he be a slut and she has to be a virgin!!!!<br><br>Jake's sob story ..............I was like......<blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480289329ra/21293382.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m6rcacOd7R1rxevt4o1_250_zpsft8gccl7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>Despite the disappointment, I am still going ahead and reading the remainder of MS books........and I can't wait.<br><br>As they say, you can't win them all..............</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_562002931" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/562002931" />
    <a title="Miss H" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h"><img alt="Miss H" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1475977422p2/15490946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/562002931?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Miss H" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Miss H" href="/user/show/15490946-miss-h">Miss H</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17608346-leo">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=badly-written">badly-written</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=needs-proper-editing">needs-proper-editing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15490946-miss-h?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer562002931" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1244255393162122085">I really wanted to love this book. However, despite its promising premise, I was disappointed. <br/><br/>Unfortunately, this book suffered from far too many editing problems. Most of the dialogue tags were punctuated incorrectly, with periods at the end of the dialogue where commas should’ve been used instead. Furthermore, you can’t speak an action. A period is needed as a separator between the action and the dialogue, not a comma.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413517ra/814309.gif' width='400' height='160' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm sorry, but I’m of the opinion that if you’re going to put your book out</span>
  <span id="freeText1244255393162122085" style="display:none">I really wanted to love this book. However, despite its promising premise, I was disappointed. <br><br>Unfortunately, this book suffered from far too many editing problems. Most of the dialogue tags were punctuated incorrectly, with periods at the end of the dialogue where commas should’ve been used instead. Furthermore, you can’t speak an action. A period is needed as a separator between the action and the dialogue, not a comma.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413517ra/814309.gif" width="400" height="160" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm sorry, but I’m of the opinion that if you’re going to put your book out on the market for people to buy, then it should be properly edited.<br><br>The writing was boring, not the mention awkward at times. Every time the two main characters spoke to each other, whether in person or on the phone, they constantly said the other person’s name. Actually, this problem wasn’t limited to just the main characters. People don’t talk like that.<br><br>The story was rife with telling instead of showing. But, not to worry, there were plenty of smutty scenes to make up for it.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/383170.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sorry, but an overabundance of smut is not a substitute for lack of plot or character development. Evie would start her day and proceed to <i>tell</i> us everything by using a heavy dose of info dumping.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413517ra/814310.gif" width="400" height="219" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both Evie and Jake were one dimensional characters. Jake was basically a watered-down version of Christian Grey, minus the whole BDSM aspect. I mean, seriously, this book even featured a female pedophile.<br><br>Evie fell in love with Jake after just knowing him a few days. Let's not forget that they met because he was stalking her. With Evie’s background, which included molestation, I found this a little hard to believe. I guess having 'chemistry' with a perfect stranger overrules common sense. Who cares about personal safety when the person stalking you is Adonis personified? She was a little too perfect, far too nice, and of course, extremely beautiful, but totally unaware of said beauty. No one let her forget these things either. People constantly praised her spectacular beauty and good-doer nature. It's like, okay, I get it. You don't have to ram it down my throat every chapter. I didn't forget. If her Mary-Sue tendencies were toned down, she could’ve been a more enjoyable character. <br><br>I wish the plot had been meatier and less predictable. I have to admit that, at times, I felt like I was reading an imitation Kristen Ashley book, slight though it may be. It was just little things here and there. Anyway, take that for what you will. All in all, though, it wasn't a bad read. Not great, but not terrible, either.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1244255393162122085" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17608346-leo">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<div id="review_559333292" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559333292" />
    <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog"><img alt="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416791332p2/4597644.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559333292?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17608346-leo">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/8652320-atran">ATran </a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=first-love-crush">first-love-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy">lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-player">lead-character-player</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=march-2013">march-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=hot-and-heavy">hot-and-heavy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=explicit">explicit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=highly-emotional">highly-emotional</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559333292" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1158433806629039242">4.5 Stars<br/><br/><b>
  <i>I look into his eyes and ask, “Why are you looking at me?”<br/>His eyes search mine for several long seconds before he hold contact and whispers, “Because I like your face.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>ATran recommended this book to me yesterday and after I read the blurb, I knew I had to read it ASAP. I luckily found it on Smashwords a day early than its scheduled release date and just dove right in. I was intrigued immediately. The story began with our H/h, Leo and Evie, only 15 and 14 respectively. The setting w</span>
  <span id="freeText1158433806629039242" style="display:none">4.5 Stars<br /><br /><b>
  <i>I look into his eyes and ask, “Why are you looking at me?”<br />His eyes search mine for several long seconds before he hold contact and whispers, “Because I like your face.” </i>
</b><br /><br />ATran recommended this book to me yesterday and after I read the blurb, I knew I had to read it ASAP. I luckily found it on Smashwords a day early than its scheduled release date and just dove right in. I was intrigued immediately. The story began with our H/h, Leo and Evie, only 15 and 14 respectively. The setting was on a rooftop, snow slowly starting to come down, not wanting to say goodbye to each other. Both children of the foster care system, Leo has been adopted and is moving. He promises to write her and come back for her when she turns eighteen so that they can begin their life together. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I’m going to kiss you now, Evie, and when I do, it’s going to mean that you’re mine. I don’t care how far away from each other we are. You. Are. Mine. I’ll wait for you. And I want you to wait for me. Promise me you won’t let anyone else touch you. Promise me you’ll save yourself for me.” </i>
</b><br /><br />Oh yea. I was SOLD. <br /><br /><i>Fast forward eight years…</i><br /><br />Evie has not heard a word from Leo. The last time she saw or heard from him was atop the roof eight years ago. She is now twenty-two and has worked hard to get where she is. She’s not rich by any means, works two jobs to pay rent, but no matter what, she is happy with her life. Knowing where she has been, she doesn’t take anything for granted. Her life is uneventful for the most part, except for the stalker that has been following her for last week and half. He doesn’t give off creepy vibes, especially since he looks harmless, and gorgeous, too. She’s actually amused at how obvious he is. She decides to confront him and find out why he’s stalking her.<br /><br />Jake is there to fulfill Leo’s dying wish: to check on Evie and make sure she’s okay. This is how Evie finds out what has happened to her Leo: A car accident claimed his life. She doesn’t really know how to process this information, nor does she understand why Jake keeps showing up after confronting him. But it’s pretty obvious that they have an immediate connection. Evie’s beauty and, most of all, her kindness, draws him in. <br /><br />The more Evie and Jake spend with each other, the more Evie falls madly for him, but she remains hesitant. Jake is holding something back. We know barely anything about him and on a few occasions, makes Evie doubt his level of honesty. What do really know about Jake? What is he hiding?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>Totally bossy. But totally sweet. And totally hot.</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Evie,” he says quietly, finally looking at me, “what I mean is, when I fuck you, you’re going to be mine. Is that clear enough for you?” </i>
</b><br /><br />I honestly couldn’t put the book down. Not only was I enjoying Jake’s bossiness and aggressiveness, but most of all I wanted to know exactly who he is. What was he not telling us? Throughout the book, I was trying to read between the lines, so to speak. I formed a theory, but nothing was confirmed until towards the end. By then, I was completely engrossed wanting to know the connection. There were times where my heart actually broke for both Evie and Jake. This is definitely an emotional story and would recommend it. But be warned, the story could’ve used a little editing, but not to the point of annoyance really, but I thought I’d just mention it anyway. Happy reading!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1158433806629039242" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1096936852?book_show_action=true">Nov 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone looking for a great love story</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=sweet-heart-warming-stories">sweet-heart-warming-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1096936852" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12871770256339300151">Wow! Why didn't I read this book a long time ago??? This story was fanfreakingtastic!<br/><br/>The chemistry between Evie and Jake was off the charts! There was just enough angst to keep the story exciting, without too much eye-roll inducing drama. Ms. Sheridan seemed to get the mix just right for an engaging, provocative story that is still believable and not overdone.The characters were well-developed and easy to relate to, despite having dark pasts. Not too short, not too long. This book was just aweso</span>
  <span id="freeText12871770256339300151" style="display:none">Wow! Why didn't I read this book a long time ago??? This story was fanfreakingtastic!<br /><br />The chemistry between Evie and Jake was off the charts! There was just enough angst to keep the story exciting, without too much eye-roll inducing drama. Ms. Sheridan seemed to get the mix just right for an engaging, provocative story that is still believable and not overdone.The characters were well-developed and easy to relate to, despite having dark pasts. Not too short, not too long. This book was just awesome!<br /><br />This was my first book by Ms. Sheridan, but definitely not my last! She is definitely getting moved up my TBR list STAT!</span>

<div id="review_559274812" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559274812" />
    <a title="J" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10343430-j"><img alt="J" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559274812?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J" href="/user/show/10343430-j">J</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559274812" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9869200504407865744"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Why are you looking at me?"<br/>"Because I like your face."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><br/><i>~Love is like a magnifying glass straight into the souls of those who own your heart.~</i><br/><br/><br/><br/>Thrown together in foster care Evie meets Leo. <br/>Through the hardships of their childhood, a deep abiding friendship blossoms. Leo becomes her protector and as the years go by this special relationship develops into a beautiful and unwavering love. <br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>~"I'm going to kiss you now, Evie, and when I do, it's going to mean that you're mine. I don</blockquote></b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText9869200504407865744" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>"Why are you looking at me?"<br>"Because I like your face."</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><i>~Love is like a magnifying glass straight into the souls of those who own your heart.~</i><br><br><br><br>Thrown together in foster care Evie meets Leo. <br>Through the hardships of their childhood, a deep abiding friendship blossoms. Leo becomes her protector and as the years go by this special relationship develops into a beautiful and unwavering love. <br><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>~"I'm going to kiss you now, Evie, and when I do, it's going to mean that you're mine. I don't care how far away from each other we are. You. Are. Mine. I'll wait for you. And I want you to wait for me. Promise me you won't let anyone else touch you. Promise me you'll save yourself for me."~Leo</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><br>When Leo suddenly gets adopted, moving across the county, Evie, is left behind. <br>Leo Promises Evie that he will write her as soon as he gets there and he will come back for her when she turns 18. <br><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413114i/812997.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <blockquote>~<b>"It will only ever be you Evie.</b><br><br><b>It's the last thing he ever says to me. I never see Leo again.~</b>
</blockquote>
</i><br><br>8 Years later Evie has made a life for herself.<br>Working 2 jobs, friends that are like the family she never had, she is happy enjoying her life, appreciating her fortune. <br><br>When a man by the name of Jake comes into her life claiming to know Leo, Evie is taken back to the mystery of what happened to Leo.<br><br>The story of Evie and Leo's past is revealed throughout the book. We are shown what they’ve been through with each other, but the reader is only given a small part of that through conversations and through flashbacks. <br><br>Jake is sent to check on Evie as a promise he made to Leo.<br>Evie and Jake have undeniable chemistry. And in such a short time, Evie is drawn to him. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>~"When he laughs like that, I swear a piece of my soul, the part of me that keeps secrets even from myself, tries to lunge towards him, like his happiness is an visible pull to my own heart. It's crazy. I don't even know this guy. ~ </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>Their relationship is smoking hot, Jake is one hot alpha male. <br>Bossy but not pushy. Totally sweet, totally hot.<br>The sex.. Omg hot hot hot hot hot! <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>~"Come for me, Evie," he growls. And just like that, my body tenses and I arch up off the couch, intense waves of ecstasy flowing through me. I cry out his name and hear his zipper and then he is flipping me over and his hands are on my hips as he drags me up so my ass is in the air and he plunges into my dripping sex on one loud moan. I'm not sure if it's his or mine or both. ~</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><br>But Jake has a past an insecurities that keeps him holding back from Evie. Inevitably the truth will always find its way. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413114i/812998.png" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <br>And just when you think you’ve figured out what happened, you get smacked down with the brutal reality, and it is heartbreakingly tragic. <br> <br>I was right all along in my suspicion of what Jake was hiding. But was totally thrown with the truth of it all. Wow didn't see that one coming. <br><br><br>Mia Sheridan is an amazing storyteller. Her writing has depth and sensitivity to it that goes beyond the words. It grabbed my attention and held it all the way through to the last word. <br>Her story made me feel that I know her personally. Not just Evie and Jake but Mia herself. <br>That's a little strange for me, I love it when I can connect to the characters and feel what they feel, and I did, but also found that when reading some things I would think, that's so Mia. LOL very crazy when I don't know her. Hahahaha <br><br>I Loved Loved loved the Epilogue. <br>I love me an epilogue and this was just perfect. <br>Leaving me with a tear escaping right as I read the last line. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>~All along she stood there constant and calm.<br>"I can't make the fire go away, I can't guarantee you won't get burned. But I can hold this hoop for you, I can remain steady and strong, because I believe in you. Because you are mine." <br>And in the end, I had jumped. And the other side was just as glorious as her eyes had promised.~</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413114i/812999.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Favorite lines <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>~"Because I like your face"~<br><br>~"I don't know if I'm ready for this huge jump in status," I tease "From stalker to chaperone in one day? You'll think I'm easy!"~<br><br>~If you're lucky, you might have a person who tells you a better story, one that takes up residence in your soul, speaking louder that the woeful tale you've convinced yourself of. If you let it speak loudly within your heart, it becomes your passion and your purpose. And this is a good thing, the best of things. because it is the very definition of love, nothing else. ~</blockquote>
</i><br><br>Can't wait to read more from this fabulous author. <br>+ 5 stars +<br><br>Buy it. <br>Read it.<br>Love it.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9869200504407865744" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Roksana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2791865-roksana"><img alt="Roksana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465938037p2/2791865.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1695175142?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1695175142" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6840341227208623306">Self Note: Upon reading this review I can see a completely different side to this story contrary to all the high rating reviews..."I hate double standards" and I want fairness, I want my heroine enjoining sexual life and not holding back and saving herself for the Hero where he on the other hand is having sex with anyone that moves! This is not sexy not desirable! This is a contemporary romance, hence it should inspire equality and not encourage double standards! Why is the heroine untouched to </span>
  <span id="freeText6840341227208623306" style="display:none">Self Note: Upon reading this review I can see a completely different side to this story contrary to all the high rating reviews..."I hate double standards" and I want fairness, I want my heroine enjoining sexual life and not holding back and saving herself for the Hero where he on the other hand is having sex with anyone that moves! This is not sexy not desirable! This is a contemporary romance, hence it should inspire equality and not encourage double standards! Why is the heroine untouched to show the depth of love for the hero, but he cannot have the same for her? Especially when he slept with lots of women for materialistic needs....basically he traded the love of his life for luxuries! Read this review, then you will understand my self-note. <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1562894423?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('wwy7RkrE6h1YTdRJ0XJW7G+r2d3s7MTxRCVEnm9iD61niQ2s2UPAriO7vPi0dqtwF8wjTRqAD39q31a4gmJX9A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('V8ZOWnV6g+YiuJJBkbxT0QQnHSki91m73uXLBv/xFcPzQ/iw5v2pVVlO+vD0uK5NfEDnudSbkjXwH9kgEvFNmg==')})
  }
